      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 15th century BC
       </b>
       . During the period 1500 to 1401 BC there were 226
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 77 were partial, 69 were annular (four
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 62 were total (one non-central), and 18 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, in 1470 BC and 1452 BC, and one month, April 1448 BC, had two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div style="clear:both;">
